 What has been the history of the seat
 
 
 
 The Buldhana Lok Sabha seat has been a Congress stronghold for over 40 years
 yahaan sabase pehle chunaav 1951 main hua tha us vakt yahaan ek seat se do saansad gopalrav bajirao khedkar or lakshmana bhatkar chunaav jitkar sansad pahunche the
 It is known that Gopalrao Bajirao Khedkar was also the first President of Maharashtra Pradesh Congress
 aapako bataa den ki buldhana loksabhaa aisi seat thi jahaan kabhi seat ek hua karti thi or saansad do the
 In fact, in the first two general elections in the country after independence, two mps from Vidarbha's Bhandara, Akola and Buldhana constituencies were elected simultaneously
 isamen ek khule pravarg se va ek arakshit (anusuchit jati) varg se chune jate the
 For this reason, two mps were elected in the general election before Buldhana
 1952 main arakshit varg se lakshmana bhatkar va khule pravarg se congress ke gopalrav khedkar chunaav jite the
 The reserved seat from Buldhana was abolished in the second general election held in 1957
 iske baad 1957 ke loksabhaa chunaav main shivaram rango rane chunaav jitkar aae
 After this, he won the elections in 1962, 1967 and reached the Lok Sabha
 lekin shivaram rango rane ke 1970 main nidhan ke baad yahaan dobaaraa loksabhaa chunaav hue
 This time too Congress came here by winning and YS Shivram won the Lok Sabha
 wo yahaan se 1971 main bhi phir chunaav jite
 When the Congress lost here for the first time in 30 years
 
 
 
 In the 1977 Lok Sabha elections, the Republic Party of India (khobragade) broke the Congress' winning streak and won Daulat Gunjaji Gavai elections for the first time here
 haalanki, iske agle hi loksabhaa chunaav yani ki balachandra ramchandra vaasanic congress ko yahaan jeet dilaane main kaamyaab rahe
 After him, son Mukul Wasnik won elections from here in 1984 on a Congress ticket
 bas ek hi baar jiti bijepi
 
 
 This seat was won by BJP for the first time in 1989
 sukhdev nanaaji kaale yahaan se chunaav jitkar pahunche
 However, in 1991, Mukul Wasnik won again and made a return to the Congress
 is baar bijepi yahaan koi kamaal nahin kar pai
 Rise of Shiv Sena
 
 
 1996 main shivasena ke aanandarav vithoba adsul buldhana loksabhaa seat par pehali baar jitkar aae or is seat par sena kaa khaataa kholaa
 Shiv Sena also spread its foot in the assembly constituencies here
 lekin 1998 ke chunaav main mukul vaasanic ne baaji palatate hue chunaav jeeta
 This was Shiv Sena's first defeat
 shivasena ne is seat par aanandarav vithoba adsul ko dobaaraa utarkar daanv khelaa
 He won in 1999, 2004
 iske baad aanandarav vithoba adsul ne amravati kii seat sanbhali or 2009 main yahaan pratap raav jadhav khadey hue
 He won this seat continuously in 2009 and 2014
 kya he vidhansabha kshetron kii sthiti

 itibipi ne apane avivaahit, virangana or jeevanasathi se alag ho chuke karmiyon ko bal ke andar hi yogya va sahi jeevanasathi dhundne main madad pahunchane ke liye ek vishesh vaivaahik portal (metrimonial portal) banaaya he

 -19 sitambar ko akhilesh yadav ne bataaya ki shivpal yadav pradesh adhyaksh rahenge
 Akhilesh Yadav was made the Chairman of the Parliamentary Board
 shivpal ke sabhi vibhaag bhi lautaae gaye
 At that time, Akhilesh Yadav reached Shivpal's house and congratulated him and said that he had gone to uncle's house, not to the president
 -19 sitambar ko shivpal yadav ne ramgopal yadav ke bhaanje or vidhaan parishad ke sadsy arvind pratap yadav ko party se nikaal diya, phir shivpal yadav ne akhilesh ke kareebi maane jane vaale kuch netaaon ko party se nikaal diya, jisamen yuva sanghathan ke adhyaksh bhi shaamil the
 These leaders were accused of making statements against Mulayam Singh Yadav
 -26 sintabar ko akhilesh yadav ne barkhaast kiye gaye mantriyon ko party main waapas liya
 Then on 7 October, the Qaumi Ekta Dal merged with the Samajwadi Party
 24 oktober ko mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav ne shivpal yadav or unke kareebi teen mantriyon ko cabinet se barkhaast kar diya tha phir isse naaraaz hokar shivpal yadav ne akhilesh yadav ke kareebi maane jane vaale ramgopal yadav ko party se chah saal ke liye barkhaast kar diya
 - On October 24, the relationship between Akhilesh Yadav and uncle Shivpal Yadav deteriorated further when Shivpal Yadav accused Akhilesh that Akhilesh had talked about forming a new party
 24 oktober ko hui party kii baithak main akhilesh or mulaayam ek-duusare par aarope lagaate hue dikhe
 At this meeting, at the behest of Mulayam Singh, Akhilesh Yadav touched Shivpal Yadav's leg and also hugged him, but after a while there was a bit of bitterness between them
 -17 november ko ramgopal yadav ko mulaayam singh yadav ne party main waapas le liya
 On December 26, Akhilesh Yadav submitted his list of 403 candidates to party president Mulayam Singh Yadav

 is press conference main khud mukhyamantri maujuud nahin the or yah mana ja rahaa tha ki akhilesh apni list jari karenge

 niyukti na hui to iske gambhir nattejey bhugatne ko taiyaar rahen
 The comments court ne kaha he ki agar aap lokayukta kii niyukti main naakaam rahete hai to ham aadesh main likhenge ki siem, governor or elahabaad hoicourt ke chif justise apni duty karne main asafal rahe
 Earlier, the Supreme Court had directed to appoint Lokayukta in UP, but till now this work has not been done
 court ne isi maheene upi ko notice jari karke lokayukta kii niyukti na karne ko lekar jawaab maanga tha

 isse purv supreme court ne nirdesh diya tha upi main lokayukta kii niyukti kii jaae, lekin ab tak yah kaary nahin hua

 pradhanmantri narendra modi ne aaj noida main dilli metro kii nai magenta line kaa udghaatan kiya

 metro kaa udghaatan karne ke liye pradhanmantri narendra modi noida ke botanical metro stesan pahunche
 He was received by UP CM Yogi Adityanath here
 is dauraan vahaan upi ke rajyapal ram nik bhi maujuud rahe
 After the Metro inauguration, PM Modi traveled in the metro with CM Yogi Adityanath
 wo botanical garden stesan se okhla bird centuri stesan tak gaye
 He was accompanied by Governor Ram Naik, CM Yogi Adityanath and local BJP MLA Pankaj Singh
 twit main magenta line kii tarifisse pehle ravivaar ko piem modi ne kaha ki dilli metro kii nav nirmit magenta line shahari parivahan ke aadhunikeekaran kii ek misaal he
 This line will make travel between Delhi and Noida faster and easier
 modi ne twit main likhaa, 'yah nai line ek or udhaaharan he ki ham kaise shahari parivahan kaa aadhunikeekaran kar rahe hai

 is saal mujhe kochi or hyderabad metro kaa udghaatan karne or usamen safar karne kaa avasar praapt hua

 dilli-noida kii yatra tej or sugam ho jaaegi

 Jitin Prasad is one of the young leaders of the Congress, he is considered close to Congress President Rahul Gandhi
 unke pita jitendra prasad bharat ke pradhanmantri rajeev gandhi(1991) or pi
 V
 narsimha raav (1994) ke raajnneetik salaahkaar rah chuke hai
 Jitendra Prasad has been the President of UP Congress Committee and also the Vice President of Indian National Congress, in such a situation, Jitin Prasad was in politics
 jitin prasad kaa janm 29 november 1973 ko upi ke shahjahanpur main hua
 He did his studies from Doon School in Dehradun
 phir vah dilli chale gaye or shriram college of commers se bikom onors kiya
 After completing his bcom, he did his MBA from IMI New Delhi
 jitin ke dada jyoti prasad congress ke netaa the or unki daadi pamela prasad kapoorthala ke royal sikh parivaar se thim
 In February 2010, Jitin Prasad married former journalist Neha Seth
 jitin prasad ne apane raajnneetik kariyar kii shuruuaat saal 2001 main kii thi
 During this time he became a secretary in the Indian Youth Congress
 iske baad 2004 main unhone apane grih loksabhaa seat shahjahanpur se 14veen loksabhaa chunaav main jeet darj kii
 In 2008, Jitin Prasad was appointed as the Union Minister of State for Steel for the first time
 iske baad 2009 main jitin prasad ne dhaurhara seat se loksabhaa chunaav ladaa or jeet hasil kii
 He has held the Ministry of Road Transport and Highways from 2009 - 18 January 2001, the Ministry of Petroleum and Natural Gas from 19 January 2011 - 28 October 2012 and the Ministry of Human Resources and Development from 28 October 2012 - May 2014
 upie sarkaar main vah kendriya rajyamantri rah chuke hai
 Jitin Prasad is once again contesting from Dhaurahra in the 2019 Lok Sabha elections
 nitish kii party jediu kaa kahana he ki mukhyamantri ne yah ghoshnaa bihar chunaav ke elaan se pehle hi kar di thi yani chunavi aachaar samhita lagu hone se pehle hi is kaarykram kii jaankaree de di gai thi
 Kumar's seven promises include providing electricity to all the villages by October next year, piping water to rural homes
 iske alaava berojgaar yuvaaon ke liye 1000 rupe kii raashi jiskaa vah 9 maheene main 2 baar phayda uthaa sakate hai
 Also, for 12th pass students, student loan through student credit card, whose interest will be paid by the government
 tippaniyan The Election Commission has not taken any action on the bjp's complaint
 jediu ke nae hording main saat vaadon ke alaava unke gathbandhan party ke lalu yadav or congress kii sonia gandhi or rahul gandhi kii tasviren bhi shaamil hai
 Kumar's seven promises include providing electricity to all the villages by October next year, piping water to rural homes
